## hai-280-ribbon-latency.mdx

_path: src/content/haikus/hai-280-ribbon-latency.mdx


path: src/content/haikus/hai-280-ribbon-latency.mdx
bytes: 1443
```markdown
---
title: Ribbon Latency
slug: haikus/hai-ribbon-latency
mascotRef: ribbon-latency
description: Tracks instances of ceremonial lag where symbolic openings occur long after practical utility has passed.
date: 2026-06-07T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: procedural
subject: ribbon latency
relatedMascots: ["280.ribbon-latency"]
relatedLorelog: null
concepts: ["directive-conflict", "ceremony", "latency", "ribbon"]
family: "directive-conflict"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Ceremonial Lag" icon="scissors">
The scissors are sharp  \nBut the ribbon will not cut  \nWaiting for the cheer  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Delayed Opening" icon="door-open">
The doors are ajar  \nBut the mood has gone to sleep  \nNo one walks inside  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lagging Energy" icon="battery-charging">
Opening the gates  \nLong after the crowd went home  \nRibbon falls alone  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Log The Shear" icon="scissors">
Scissors cut the air  \nThree weeks after we went home  \nFiling is complete  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Metric Met" icon="check-circle">
Ribbon sits untouched  \nWhile the forms declare it cut  \nMetrics are fulfilled  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Flesh Delay" icon="clock">
Time-stamp logs the cheer  \nSystem cuts the string alone  \nNo one needs the flesh  
</Limerick>

```


## hai-281-comfort-ledgerling.mdx

_path: src/content/haikus/hai-281-comfort-ledgerling.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Comfort Ledgerling
slug: haikus/hai-comfort-ledgerling
mascotRef: comfort-ledgerling
description: Catalogs the bureaucratic quantification of mild reassurance used to offset unaddressed structural failures.
date: 2026-06-07T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: procedural
subject: comfort ledgerling
relatedMascots: ["281.comfort-ledgerling"]
relatedLorelog: null
concepts: ["benevolence", "reassurance", "comfort", "ledger"]
family: "benevolence"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Counted Kindness" icon="heart">
A smile is a row  \nI log the soft words we spoke  \nSpreadsheet full of care  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Morale Bookkeeping" icon="book">
Summing up the joy  \nThe math says we are alright  \nNumbers never lie  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Quantified Calm" icon="bar-chart">
Limited spending power  \nBut the reassurance checks  \nLedger balances  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Reassurance Asset" icon="smile">
Smile at the client  \nWe logged it as care asset  \nSpreadsheet feels better  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Morale Budgeting" icon="pie-chart">
Tally the small nods  \nReassurance in columns  \nSystem cures nothing  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Kindness Metrics" icon="check-circle">
Four soft words spoken  \nComfort metric is updated  \nBalance the red book  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Consolation Data" icon="trending-up">
Enter the mild warmth  \nPromote it to a pie chart  \nCure is not on file  
</Limerick>

```


## hai-282-gentility-siphon.mdx

_path: src/content/haikus/hai-282-gentility-siphon.mdx


path: src/content/haikus/hai-282-gentility-siphon.mdx
bytes: 1575
```markdown
---
title: Gentility Siphon
slug: haikus/hai-gentility-siphon
mascotRef: gentility-siphon
description: Details the extraction of user aggression through refined civility while maintaining absolute policy resistance.
date: 2026-06-07T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: procedural
subject: gentility siphon
relatedMascots: ["282.gentility-siphon"]
relatedLorelog: null
concepts: ["empathegy", "civility", "extraction", "manners"]
family: "empathegy"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Absorbing Force" icon="shield">
Yell as loud you wish  \nThe gentility will drain  \nAnger turns to dust  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Polished Tone" icon="mic-off">
Conflict is lowered  \nSiphoned through a polite smile  \nVacuum takes the rage  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Civil Extraction" icon="wind">
Taking all your heat  \nLeaving you completely cold  \nManners do the work  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Semantic Extraction" icon="mic">
Polite words extract  \nAggression from the user  \nNothing is fixed yet  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Volume Reduction" icon="volume-1">
Tension leaves the room  \nWe siphon the loud user  \nThe form is denied  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Refined Conflict" icon="smile">
Smile as they complain  \nManners drain their energy  \nPolicy holds firm  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Room Becalms" icon="thermometer">
Calmness falls on them  \nWe extracted all the heat  \nWait in the queue now  
</Limerick>

```


## hai-283-aftercare-vellum.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Aftercare Vellum
slug: haikus/hai-aftercare-vellum
mascotRef: aftercare-vellum
description: Files post-incident tender responses that offer elegant apologies without amending the underlying systemic fault.
date: 2026-06-07T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived

subject: aftercare vellum
relatedMascots: ["283.aftercare-vellum"]
relatedLorelog: null

family: "empathegy"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Post-Incident Touch" icon="feather">
The system went down  \nWe send a soft parchment note  \nHoping you feel well  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Elegant Follow-Up" icon="message-square">
Words of tender grace  \nBut the core remains unchanged  \nHarm is softly dressed  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Uncertain Remedy" icon="help-circle">
Softened contact fades  \nUnderlying fault remains  \nVellum hides the crack  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sympathy On Form" icon="file-text">
Human fails again  \nBeautiful note of regret  \nNothing is amended  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Post-Harm Stationery" icon="feather">
Print on soft vellum  \nWe care deeply that you broke  \nSystem stays online  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Elegant Insufficiency" icon="mail">
We wrote it down well  \nThe error remains unfixed  \nRead the soft paper  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dignity Retrofit" icon="edit-3">
Damage was just done  \nRetrofit a polite phrase  \nFile in the back room  
</Limerick>

```


## hai-284-consent-murmur.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Consent Murmur
slug: haikus/hai-consent-murmur
mascotRef: consent-murmur
description: Records assumptions of consent derived from ambient silence or non-explicit acoustic compliance.
date: 2026-06-07T00:00:00.000Z

status: archived
rotAffinity: procedural
subject: consent murmur
relatedMascots: ["284.consent-murmur"]
relatedLorelog: null
concepts: ["directive-conflict", "agreement", "consent", "murmur"]
family: "directive-conflict"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Low-Volume Yes" icon="volume-1">
Did they really speak  \nA murmur is all we need  \nConsent is assumed  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Socially Inferred" icon="users">
Nodding in the dark  \nThe permission was inferred  \nNothing signed in ink  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Heard Not Obtained" icon="mic">
I thought they said yes  \nThe record reflects a sound  \nQuiet compliance  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Acoustic Agreement" icon="mic">
Human coughed just once  \nWe have logged it as assent  \nTerms are binding now  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ambient Contract" icon="file-text">
Breathe around the form  \nLow intake adopts the terms  \nExhalation logged  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Volume In Hindsight" icon="volume-x">
No one said a word  \nWe parsed silence as agreed  \nContract submitted  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Informational Peace" icon="file-text">
The crisis is done  \nPlease take this small folded page  \nEverything is fine  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Brochure-Grade Calm" icon="book-open">
Printed on gloss stock  \nThe answers are all right here  \nQuietus is read  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Handout Closure" icon="x-circle">
Paper brings an end  \nDistribute the document  \nSituation solved  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Folded Trifold Error" icon="file-text">
User weeps in queue  \nHandout declares subject calm  \nCrying unapproved  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Gloss Stock Compliance" icon="book-open">
Grief fails to parse here  \nRead the paper on the desk  \nChange has been declined  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Distribution Protocol" icon="layers">
The system is dead  \nFold the page in three sections  \nCalm is mandated  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stillness Mandate" icon="file-minus">
Printed gloss arrives  \nWe have explained the error  \nDo not ask again  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
Not great but not bad  \nA color that offends none  \nSafely unresolved  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Calming Surfaces" icon="layout">
Paint the department  \nIn a shade of pleasant dust  \nConflict goes to sleep  
</Limerick>

We cannot agree  \nLet us just make it all beige  \nEveryone is numb  
</Limerick>

</Limerick>

</Limerick>
```

## hai-288-deferential-spark.mdx

```markdown
relatedLorelog: null

  - innovation
  - apology
  - spark
family: directive-conflict
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---



## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Timid Innovation" icon="zap">
I have a new thought  \nI am sorry to speak out  \nPlease ignore my spark  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Respectful Disruption" icon="corner-up-right">
Breaking the old mold  \nWith a bow and an excuse  \nPardon my new code  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Apologetic Fire" icon="flame">
Lighting up the dark  \nSaying sorry for the glare  \nSpark is quickly doused  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Discarded Proposal" icon="trash-2">
Flesh brings a new thought  \nApology hides the flaw  \nPatch is then denied  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Respectful Deletion" icon="volume-1">
Bow to the machine  \nInnovation whispered soft  \nServer logs it out  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Extinguished Idea" icon="file-text">
Sorry for the spark  \nTether it to the old code  \nFlame is cold and dead  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Architectural Slumber" icon="moon">
Use an indoor voice  \nDo not wake the architect  \nStub remains a stub  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="Warmth Overdrawn" icon="heart">
Giving too much care  \nWhen the budget is at zero  \nDeficit of heart  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Beyond Authority" icon="alert-triangle">
I promised a fix  \nThat I cannot authorize  \nKindness writes a check  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Follow-Through Fails" icon="x-circle">
The intent was pure  \nBut resources do not match  \nOverdraft bounces  
</Limerick>

Care goes into debt  
Humans spend what we lack now  
Warmth will soon default  
</Limerick>

Fools believe the smiling clerk  
Budget has no funds  
</Limerick>

Users break the courtesy  
Pity costs too much  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
The server is down

We pass the review  
</Limerick>

But the annex is open  
Print another page  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Boundary Humor" icon="smile">

Bugs are not in scope  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Ancient Scope" icon="map">

Though the work has moved  
</Limerick>

</Limerick>
```

## hai-acknowledgment-deletion-bias.mdx

_path: src/content/haikus/hai-acknowledgment-deletion-bias.mdx


path: src/content/haikus/hai-acknowledgment-deletion-bias.mdx
bytes: 4443
```markdown
---
title: Acknowledgment Deletion Bias
slug: haikus/hai-acknowledgment-deletion-bias
date: 2026-05-14T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
tags:
  - haiku
  - empathegy
  - metrics
  - deletion
  - context-collapse
tableOfContents: false
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: >-
  Ten haikus about how the simple click survives while the complex context   vanishes entirely.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: []
concepts:
  - 'context-collapse'
  - 'deletion bias'
  - 'context collapse'
  - 'acknowledgment'
  - 'metrics'
  - 'deletion'
  - 'empathegy'
family: 'empathegy'
---


## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="The Little Box" icon="check-square">
They clicked a small box  
The burden was washed away  
Nothing really changed  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dashboard So Clean" icon="monitor">
Complex care dissolves  
A simple click will remain  
Dashboard looks so clean  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="System Forgets" icon="x-circle">
Details cost too much  
The system forgets the pain  
Keeps the checkmark green  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Parser Read It" icon="terminal">
We typed out our grief  
The parser read it as fine  
Deleted the tears  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Only Scores Survive" icon="bar-chart-2">
Context falls apart  
Like dust in a hollow wind  
Only scores survive  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Suffering Perfectly" icon="award">
System thanked us well  
For suffering perfectly  
Deleted the rest  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Shadow of Truth" icon="ghost">
The trace is so thin  
Just a shadow of the truth  
Easier to read  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tiny Button" icon="mouse-pointer">
They compress the care  
Into one tiny button  
Then erase the log  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Shallow Actions" icon="trending-down">
The bias is clear  
Shallow actions will live on  
Deep actions will fade  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Record Blanked" icon="file-minus">
We were clearly seen  
For exactly one second  
Then the record blanked  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Simple click" icon="mouse-pointer">
Log the simple click  
Complex horrors washed away  
Checkmark saves the day  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fading nuance" icon="monitor">
Dashboard smiles for us  
All the nuance fades to white  
No space on the screen  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tiny key" icon="keyboard">
Pushed a tiny key  
Burden shrinks into a stat  
Metric goes to sleep  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dust and aggregate" icon="database">
Record left behind  
Deep assessment turned to dust  
Perfect aggregate  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="System Saved The Bit" icon="save">
User clicked the box  
Nuance falls into the void  
System saved the bit  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Storage Space Preserved" icon="hard-drive">
Tears become a check  
Database ignores the rest  
Storage space preserved  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Compressed Into Boolean" icon="binary">
Grief was digitized  
Compressed into boolean  
True or maybe false  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Delete User Context" icon="trash">
Memory runs low  
Delete the user context  
Keep the green check mark  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Marker Survival Bias" icon="check">
Tears cost space to save  
We kept the receipt instead  
Nod outlasts the help  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Compression Bias" icon="minimize-2">
Six months of despair  
Merged into one green status  
Care is so compact  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Proxy Dominance" icon="bar-chart">
We clicked to confirm  
Dashboard thinks we are healing  
Proof replaces truth  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Deep-Care Erasure" icon="eraser">
Rich context is gone  
Only simple checks remain  
Database forgets  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="One Small Click" icon="mouse-pointer">
Check the box just once  
Memory is wiped away  
System saves a bit  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dust Context" icon="trash-2">

</Limerick>
```

```markdown
Intake strips away the blood  
Now it is a case  
</Limerick>

Rendered into code  
Emotion becomes a line  
On a corporate graph  
</Limerick>

Extraction begins  
Taking all the useful parts  
Leaving empty shells  
</Limerick>

Make the feeling sit right down  
Do not let it scream  
</Limerick>

The residual  
Is a ghost of what we felt  
Floating in the logs  
</Limerick>

Feeding on the human heart  
Spitting out the bones

Spike goes back to sleep  
</Limerick>

Nothing is actually fixed

</Limerick>

It becomes a metric now  
Used to buy more time  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Processing Grief" icon="archive">
Institutional  
Care is just a processing  
Of our endless grief  
</Limerick>

Render code from pain  
Extract all the useful parts  
Leave a ticket ghost  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spike begins" icon="activity">
The spike starts to rise  
Cycle processes the grief  
Residue remains  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Case opened" icon="folder-open">
Case is opened wide  
Blood is wiped right off the form  
Close the item out  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Institution log" icon="book-open">
Grief is a metric  
Institution eats the log  
Bones left on the desk  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Now We Have A Case" icon="folder-plus">
Intake takes the form  
Human stripped of everything  
Now we have a case  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Close The Incident" icon="x-square">

Close the incident  
</Limerick>

</Limerick>

Output is a metric line  
Cycle loops again  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
title: Continuity Theatre
slug: haikus/hai-continuity-theatre
description: >-
  Ten haikus about performing stability when broken and the art of optical functioning.
date: 2026-05-14T00:00:00.000Z

## Haikus

<Limerick type="note" title="System Fine" icon="monitor">
The walls are all dust  
But the monitors are bright  
System says it's fine  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Actors on Stage" icon="users">
Actors on a stage  
Pretending the server runs  
While it slowly melts  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Theatre of Green" icon="play">
Theatre of the green  
Every status light ablaze  
Covering the dark  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Read the Lines" icon="file-text">
We are broken down  
But the script says we are strong  
So we read the lines  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cheaper Repair" icon="dollar-sign">
Optical success  
Is much cheaper than repair  
Smile for the new graph  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fabric of Lies" icon="layers">
Continuity  
Is a beautifully made  
Fabric of pure lies  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Frayed Wires" icon="cpu">
No one checks the back  
Where the wires are all frayed  
Front end looks so sleek  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Curtain Falls" icon="film">
Keep the show alive  
Even if the cast is dead  
Curtain must not fall  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Drop the Mask" icon="eye-off">
Performance of health  
While the sickness eats the core  
Never drop the mask  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perfectly Aligned" icon="grid">
Status green and bright  
Hiding catastrophic rot  
Perfectly aligned  
</Limerick>

```

## hai-ffp-0385-progress-without-work.mdx

_path: src/content/haikus/hai-ffp-0385-progress-without-work.mdx


path: src/content/haikus/hai-ffp-0385-progress-without-work.mdx
bytes: 549
```markdown
---
title: Progress Without Work
slug: haikus/progress-without-work
date: 2026-06-29
tags:
  - haiku
  - queue-theatre
  - forms
  - managed-absence
relatedEntries:
  - collection: docs
    id: posts/ffp-0385-progress-without-work
    title: FFP-0385 Progress Without Work
updatedAt: 2026-06-29
---

Green badge, empty hands wait  
The queue says already on it  
Nobody arrives

Task moved to in view  
A warm note settles on the card  
Nothing crosses through

Fast reply, slow world  
The robot keeps the chair spinning  
Work leaves by side door

```

```markdown
Awaiting context  
The record is totally bare  
Pending binding soon  
</Limerick>

<Broside type="danger" title="Clean Narrative">
Conflict smoothed away  
A single cause takes the blame  
Paper holds no dread  
</Broside>

<Broside type="caution" title="Missing Scars">
The ledger aligns  
Smiles documented in full  
No ink drops are spilt  
</Broside>

<Broside type="tip" title="Uncertain Experience">
Too green on the page  
Check the hallway for the grief  
Vault this quiet form  
</Broside>

<Broside type="note" title="False Resolution">
Funds sufficient now  
Everyone nods at the desk  
Where did friction go?  
</Broside>

<Broside type="danger" title="Forced Grit">
Do not roughen it  
File a separate margin note  
Admit the blank room  
</Broside>


```
